The following is an index of each XML element and attribute used in the [XML format](https://github.com/usnistgov/OSCAL/blob/v1.0.2/xml/schema/oscal_ssp_schema.xsd) for this [model](/concepts/layer/implementation/ssp/). Each entry in the index lists all uses of the given element or attribute in the format, which is linked to the corresponding entry in the [XML Format Reference](../xml-reference/). Each entry also lists the formal name for the given element or attribute which is linked to the corresponding XML type in the [XML Format Metaschema Reference](../xml-definitions/).
